< userid>
106897184621468921307< /userid>
< Text>
The food is good, but the wait to get it was very, very long. To fill a cup with water, you leave the cafe itself and trek down a long, chilly hallway to a shared water filter in a remote part of the overall building that houses the cafe and several other businesses. (Couldn't the cafe fill some pitchers or another type of container?)  Decor is fun--reusued doors hung high to soften and disguise the high, warehouse-like ceiling strung with HVAC tubes and wiring; bright green (but plastic) ferns and draping succulents. We ordered avo toast with eggs and a Mexican bowl; tasty and, save the egg, all plant-based. Just hadn't anticipated waiting 30 minutes for this quick bite.<//Text>

< text>
One word: lovely. It's essentially a little Italian trattoria taken out of Rome and planted in the middle of Noe Valley. Despite the spacious multi-level floor, Lupa is able to create intimacy due to its warm and low-lit environment.

I never, ever finish pasta dishes because they never quite strike the balance between portion size and richness, but my Toretelloni alla Cardinale hit it right on the spot. Loved the addition of peas and prosciutto to creamy pink sauce.

Melted smoked mozzarella with mix saut√©ed mushroom appetizer is a must-try. It is smoky, cheesy, delicate, and umami. The cheese has an amazing saucy texture almost like a burrata. I've never seen anything of its kind at other Italian places.

Take a break from bustling North Beach or SOMA's trendy Italian eateries and come here. Service is impeccable as well.< /text>

< Review>
We got our heat pump/furnace installed about 3 weeks ago. On day one it was not working properly since the wrong part was installed. Who doesn't check parts before its installed? The crew left handprints on our wall, doors and staircase, they were NOT wearing gloves when I was reassured they would wear gloves. They chipped a part of our closet door and stained our pavers in the backyard. Paul let the oil spill all over the pavers and when confronted he was nonchalant about it, which is quite unprofessional. Once I received the bill it was incorrect and they were charging us $500 more than what we signed on the contract.

Kevin did try to make things right as best he can, though Brooke is in charge of scheduling and trying to get our pavers cleaned up. She has not offered to fix our closet door. Now, we are about 3 weeks out and we still do not have an ETA of when Craig (Bates Clean and Seal) is coming out to look at the pavers, let alone a date on when it will be cleaned. The last time I spoke to Brooke, it sounded like she forgot about scheduling him to come out. We are still missing 2 vent grills that was 'delayed due to covid'.

The company is BBB and Diamond certified, and we went with them because of their service and 'expertise' though that has not been our experience. Not all of their technicians are NATE certified, and only 80% needs to be certified. This whole experience has been a disappointment and we are still waiting for Moore Mechanical to make things right. If it wasn't for Kevin and for the Carrier system, I would have given them 1 star.<//Review>

< review>
I really wanted to write a 5 star review, but this isn't that review. Suffice to say there was plenty of reason to see why some have truly great experiences with Moore. A lot of ours fell into that. That said, communication - particularly once the main install part of our work was done - was beyond abysmal. I was left with a impression of people that have great smiles and do great work, but are not dependable. If it isn't the big commitment, it would seem to be noise and fall off the radar.

Super nutshell version: Great people, probably all well intended, but communication before the install was "OK", and communication post install - including for commitments made but not yet completed - is essentially non-existent. The install portion of our overall work was rock solid subject to one significant communication issue. If you asked us on the last installation day our rating, it would have been 5 stars. It dropped to three based on what didn't happen from then on (non-install work is part of the equation, promises to follow up and then <crickets> is most of the rest).

Synopsis version:
The Pros:
The people are all great. Extremely friendly - literally every one of them.
The installation work was tidy, done on time, and they cleaned up afterward.

The Cons:
The Consult we received seemed good at the time, but was functionally never finished. It was supposed to provide a list of specific recommendations and a quote to address them and was due to be received "in 2-3 days". We're approaching 2 months and, with multiple follow ups on our part, don't have it and do not expect to ever receive it.
We had an expected issue with line of sight to one of the ductless heads for the new heat pump. No knock at face value, but the issue was substantially worse than expected, and the communication around that was essentially non-existent. Instead of "You have to hold the remote up high", it became "You have to hold it up high while on the top of a ladder." We had a solution planned that solved both cases, so this didn't have to be a big deal. Unfortunately, there was no indication that it had went from "Important to do" to "System is functionally unusable until you do it" without so much as a word spoken about it. It's solved, but it was one of several communication misses. I discovered it when I went to turn on the unit in there and had to go fish a tall step ladder out to do it.
We followed up on both of the above cons about two weeks post install. I received a response that varied between what amounts to "Your fault not ours" (my words, not theirs, but that's what it amounted to) and "I'll have to look into that since we don't do that kind of work anymore" (the kind of work they were late estimating for us). We provided requested feedback a few weeks after that and got an email from Steve Moore the next morning saying he thought there was still room for communication. OK, I responded indicating that I wasn't sure whether there was anything to discuss if they didn't do the work anymore and the other issue we had already resolved, but that open to that if he thought it would be a productive use of both our time, and provided two time windows I could be available. No reply. I followed up again a week later to see if he was still interested in that chat - again, no reply. I guess he wasn't... ;)

The Neutral:
The jury is still out on the design. The most core item being addressed seems to be doing great. The question mark is elsewhere and is based on things I've learned since the install. I don't pretend to be an expert and knowing for sure will take both more information and some time, so don't treat that one as good or bad - just unknown)</review>

< review>
Overall they provided a very good product and service at a fair price. I was pleasantly surprised when they contacted me to say I had a free inspection due to my recently installed split system, something I was not aware of but was apparently included with the purchase of the original install. I agreed and a date was set. I was told the technician would arrive between 8 and 12 that morning, and I would receive a notice when the technician was on the way. I waited all morning, no notice, and no technician. Finally he arrived mid afternoon, I did not receive a text nor a phone call alerting me that he was on the way. He did his job and left. He seemed thorough and professional. Before he left I asked if he needed me to sign anything. He said "No". So, I signed nothing in regard to his visit.

I did not score 5 stars for the following reason; At the end of the day I checked my email account and found an email posted that afternoon from Moore Mechanical saying the technician was on his way. Unlike some people who have their noses stuck in a device all day 24/7, I do not. I have better things to do other than constantly monitor my computer for emails. I check emails first thing in the morning, and again after dinner. I go about my day doing more productive things. In this case I was expecting a telephone call alerting me the technician was on his way, not an email notice. So, in that regard there was a breakdown in communication as to when the technician was going to show up.

Last; Moore Mechanical sent me an invoice by email as a result of this inspection visit. It showed a $179.00 service was performed for free. Okay! At least I received in writing that I owed nothing for this inspection. The invoice included more than one page of legalese describing contractor's licensing laws, and language stating that I understand  these laws and inspected the technicians work at the conclusion of his visit. The form said I agree the technician did all service and repairs in a correct and professional manner. I then see what appears to be my signature at the bottom of these documents, dated the same day as the inspection.

For the record I did not sign that form. It appears to be an electronic signature transposed from some other document I may have previously signed years ago back when I first purchased the install. I don't necessarily disagree with anything stated in the recent invoice documents, but I did not sign anything for the technician, nor on line, as part of this free service offered by Moore Mechanical.

I'm not saying that I don't appreciate the free follow up inspection to their equipment and work... I Do! What I'm saying is 'that is not my signature' on their invoice. I did not watch the technician every minute as he went about doing his task. He spent about a half hour, inside and out, doing whatever he was doing. For all I know he could have been eating his lunch. I had faith he was doing what he was supposed to do, but did not watch him do it.

I will definitely use, and recommend Moore Mechanical in the future. I feel they are a good company, and did a good install of a good product for me. I do suggest to them they use a different notification system to alert customers the technician is on the way, and to acquire a real customer signature at the time of service when documents need to be signed.< /review>

<userid>102522020879970586230</userid><Name>Trishonna James</Name><Date>1506636086213</Date><rating>5< /rating><Review>I was in an auto accident in February of this year, 2017 and was referred to Wellness Chiropractic and another Chiropractor.

At 19 I was in an auto accident, and at 27 I was in another auto accident that left me disabled for 7 years. During that time I tried to get help from Chiropractors from all over. I eventually saw a NUCCA Chiropractor (National Upper Cervical Chiropractic Association). I was diagnosed with a post-traumatic upper cervical subluxation. They told me I had pressure on my brainstem and the pinching of an artery going to my brain. For two years they tried to correct it to no avail. I would pop out of alignment with in days or sometime even hours after my adjustment. After two years my adrenals were shot. I was told my subluxation was so bad it was like trying to balance a bowling ball on top of a golf tee pin. So after 4 years of Chiropractic treatment and not wanting surgery, I gave up and thought I would have to live with this problem for life. I turned to massage which helped me survive.
Then miracle of all miracles I met Brian this year. He was confident he could help me. He wasn't concerned that my atlas and access was misaligned or that no one had been able to get it corrected for me. He told me, "We won't worry about your atlas till a little later. I want to start by working from the ground up so to speak. Let's make sure your hips are aligned and you are standing correctly. Then we will address your neck." I was impressed to say the least.
I felt a confidence and competence in Brian's hands I had never experienced before. It was my sixth visit before he finally adjusted my atlas and WOW... what a huge release of energy that flowed through my body when the years of pinching on my brainstem was over. And would you believe it, the adjustment stayed put and has never popped out since. If I were to go into the details of the physiological changes my body has gone through and the depths of my recovery I could write a book. But let me just say, I went in with reverse curve of my lumbar, thoracic and cervical spine. After seeing him two times a week from March through August, I am now enjoying better health than I have in the last 20 years. Everything has been corrected and aligned properly. I have never felt better. I can not say enough good about Brian. He is the best; God's gift to humanity in my humble opinion. If I could give him 10 gold stars I would. <text>Service was great price affordable. Got their spicy chicken sandwich and a three piece. The chicken in the sandwich was a little sparse but the flavor was good. The pickles are a tad mild even with the extra I ordered they didn't really come through like Popeyes, but sauce and dense texture of the bun was a plus. The three piece consisted of 2 legs and a "breast". Ask for a thigh, you'll get better value. Their breasts lose some of the meat to the wings and are a bit small. The spicy chicken has an awesome kick and real heat that comes on slow. It also came with a honey butter biscuit which was somewhere between a biscuit and a chewy roll. The crisp of this particular location remained even after sitting for 45 minutes in a box and didn't get greasy like other franchises I've been to. Would definitely go again.<//text><Resp>None< /Resp>< date>
